 jahrili ho chuki dilli kii hawa ke vifaille prabhaav ko kam karne ke liye aap sarkaar ne ye skim lagu kii he
 The government hopes that this formula will reduce the number of vehicles on the streets of Delhi, so the smoke will also be reduced and the already dangerously dangerous Delhi air will remain somewhat breathable
 simple he od-ivan kaa ganitand-ivan system dilli main teesri baar lagu kiya he
 So you will definitely get some familiarity with this system
 phir bhi ham aapako vistaar se bataate hai ki koun si taarikh ko kis number kii car lekar aap dilli kii sadakon par nikalen taaki aapako baari-bharkam jurmaana na bharna pade
 If the last number of your car's number plate is even, that is, 2,4,6,8,0 is written there, then you will be able to remove your car on the 4th, 6th, 8th, 10th, 12th and 14th
 agar aapaki gaadi ke number plate kaa aakhri number od yani bisham sankhya he, yani ki 1,3,5,7,9 he to aap 5, 7, 9, 11, 13 or 15 taarikh ko apni car se dilli kii sadakon par farrata bhar sakenge
 So today is number 4, and if the number of the car you have is 2,4,6,8,0, then you go out on the streets of Delhi without worry

 Earlier in 2016, this scheme has been implemented twice
 ise pehali baar 1 janvari se lekar 15 janvari tak lagu kiya gaya tha or dobaaraa 16 april se lekar 30 april tak
 The rebate given to them will also be applicable on cnc-powered vehicles including the odd-even system petrol and diesel
 yahi nahin agar aap haryana, upi yaa bharat ke kisi anya rajya se bhi car lekar dilli aate hai to aapako is niyam kaa paalan karnaa hoga
 The only woman traveling in a car or going with a school child will be exempt from the odd even rule
 iske alaava electric kaaron par bhi od ivan niyam lagu nahin hoga
 The Delhi government has also exempted two-wheelers from this rule
 iske alaava ravivaar 10 november ko bhi ye niyam lagu nahin hoga
 This means that both Aud and Even numbers will be able to run on this day
 padhein: damaghontu hawa ke bich swasthya mantri kaa twit, gaajar khaaie pradooshan ke khataron ko dur bhagieis niyam se apatkaaleen sevaaon jaise ambulance, fire sarvice ko chhot milegi
 The vehicles of the President, Vice President and Prime Minister are also outside the scope of this rule
 iske alaava divyangon ko bhi niyam se chhot dene kaa faisla kiya gaya he
 If the rule is broken then it is not a huge penalty that the aud even rule will be applicable round the clock

 500 atirikt basen daudengeenyatriyon ko od-ivan skim ke dauraan kisi tarah kii dikkat na ho iske liye dilli sarkaar ne 500 extra bason kii vyavastha kii he
 These buses will run on different routes, so that more and more riders can benefit from it
 zyada charge nahin kar sakengin ola-ubarrajdhani main ap ke jariye car muhaiyaa karaane vaali companiyon main shaamil ola-ubar kai baar peak aavar main zyada demand kaa phayda uthaati hai or savaariyon se zyada kiraaya charge karti hai, bijness kii bhashaa main ise sarj prising kehete hai
 But during aud even system these companies will not be able to charge you much rent
 dilli sarkaar ne in companiyon se pehle hi is baavat baat kar lee he

 is vajah se badi sankhya main offis jane vaale log sadakon par niklenge
 In this regard, the arrangements of Delhi Government and traffic departments are also tested today

 kendriya vitt mantri nirmala sitaamaran aaj modi sarkaar 2
 Going to present the first budget of 0
 ise 'new india' kaa bajet kaha ja rahaa he jiske jariye modi sarkaar sust padi arthvyavastha kii gati tej karne ke upaay kar sakati he
 The corporate-industry is eyeing this budget, the most common eye is that of the common man who is worried about unemployment and incomes not increasing
 kuch hi ghanton main vitt mantri nirmala sitaamaran apana bajet bhaashan shuru karengi, lekin ise samajhnaa aapke liye mushkil na ho, iske liye ham lekar aae hai, bajet kii shabdaawalee aasaan shabdon main
 Understand these words, it will become easy for you to understand the budget
 1
 Tax (tax): The government makes income from tax to meet its expenses
 yah ek prakaar kaa anivaary bhugtan he jise karadaata ko sarkaar ko dena hota he
 There are two types of this tax, direct tax and indirect tax
 vah tex, jise aapse sidhe taur par vasula jaataa he, jaise inakam tex, corporate tex, share yaa duusari sampattiyon se aay par kar, property tex aadi diarect tex yaa pratyaksh kar kehalaate hai
 On the other hand, the tax which is not taken directly from the public but whose burden ultimately falls on it, is called indirect tax
 jaise, desh main taiyaar kii gai vastuon par lagane vaala utpaada shulk (exise), aayaat yaa niryaat kiye jane vaale vastuon par lagane vaale seemaa shulk (custom), sarvice tex aadi apratyaksh kar hai
 2 Cess and Surcharge: Cess or Cess is levied only on a tax base to raise money for a particular purpose with a tax
 jaise svachh bharat ses, krishi kalyaan ses, svachh paryaavaran ses aadi
 Surcharge or surcharge is a tax levied which is calculated on the basis of tax liability
 saamanytah ise inakam tex ke upar lagaaya jaataa he
 3
 iskar (income tax):yah hamaari aay ke strot jaise ki aamadani, nivesh or us par milane vaale byaaj par lagata he
 4
 corporate tex (corporate tax):corporate tex corporate sansthaanon yaa fermon par lagaaya jaataa he, jiske jariye sarkaar ko aamadani hoti he
 5
 utpaada shulk (excise duties):desh kii seemaa ke bheetar banane vaale sabhi utpaadon par lagane vaala tex ko utpaada shulk kehete hai
 Excise duty has now been included in GST
 6
 Customs duties: Customs duties are imposed on goods that are imported into the country or exported outside the country
 7
 Fiscal year: The financial year in India starts from April 1 and runs till March 31 of the following year
 is saal kaa bajet vittiya varsh 2019-20 ke liye hoga jo ek april 2019 se 31 march 2020 tak ke liye hoga
 There has been a demand that the financial year should be done from January to December, but it has not been accepted yet
 8
 Short-term and long-term gains: Any person in the stock market who makes a profit by investing money for less than one year is called a short-term capital gain
 sheyaron main jo paisa ek saal se adhik samay ke liye hota he use dirghakaalik puunjigat laabh (long turm capital gen) kehete hai
 Earlier there was a provision for not paying tax on long-term capital gains, but in the budget of 2018-19, 10 percent tax was made on it
 haalanki, yah tex sirf 1 lakh rupee se adhik kii kamai par hi dena hota he
 9
 sabsidi (subsidies):aarthik asamanta dur karne ke liye sarkaar kii ore se aam logon ko diya jane vaala aarthik laabh sabsidi kaha jaataa he
 For example, the government subsidizes LPG cylinders to the gas-filling poor and makes them cheaper
 yah nakad bhi ho saktaa he, lekin ab zyaadaatar sabsidi debiti ke dwaara yani sidhe labhaarthi ke khate main daalaa jaataa he
 Subsidies to companies are given as tax exemption to increase industrial activity and generate employment
 10
 Fiscal Policy and Fiscal Deficit: It is a policy that provides for government income, public expenditure (defense, health, education, electricity, roads etc
), tax rates (direct and indirect)
 , Public debt is related to deficit financing
 sarkaar kii kul salanaa aamadani ke mukaable jab kharch adhik hota he to use rajkoshiya ghaataa kehete hai
 Since the budgetary deficit does not accurately convey the debt obligations of the government, the fiscal deficit system was introduced
 ise kuch log vittiya ghaataa bhi kehete hai
 11
 bajet ghaataa (budgetary deficit):bajet ghaataa kii sthiti tab paidaa hoti he jab kharche, rajasav se adhik ho jate hai
 It does not include the debt liability of the government
 bajtary ghaataa = kul prapti – kul vyay
 12
 sakal gharelu utpaada (gdp):sakal gharelu utpaada yani jidipi ek vittiya varsh main desh kii seemaa ke bheetar utpaadit kul vastuon or sevaaon kaa kul jod hota he
 In a way, it is considered the size of the entire economy and the rate of growth in it is considered as the rate of growth of the economy
 bharat kii jidipi vruddhi dar pichley vitt varsh main 6
 8 percent
 13
 Consolidated Fund: This is the Government of India fund that includes all the revenue receipts of the government, treasury bills issued by the government and loans recovered
 14
 Contingency Fund: An amount is kept in this fund to meet contingency expenses
 isse vyay aise muddon par kiya jaataa he jinako taala nahi ja saktaa he lekin baad main sansad se anumati lekar sanchit nidhi se rupaya lekar isamen daal diya jaataa he
 This fund holds the power of the President in relation to the Governor and Center in the States
 15
 Revenue Receipts: Receipts, which are not the responsibility of the government to pay back or are not associated with the sale of any property, are called revenue receipts
 in praptiyon ke kaaran sarkaar kii deyta (liability) main badhat nahi hoti he
 They can be divided into tax revenue (income tax, corporate tax, GST etc
) and non-tax revenue (interest, fees, dividends)
 16 
 Capital Receipts: Such public receipts are called capital receipts which increase the government's liabilities and decrease the assets of the government
 jaise desh ke andar liya gaya karj, videsh se liya gaya karj, reserve bank se liya jane vaala karj aadi
 17
 rajasav vyay (revenue Expenditure):iske andar un kharchon ko rakhaa jaataa he jisase sarkaar kii na to utpaadan kshamta kaa vistaar hota he or na hi bhavishya ke liye atirikt aay srujit hoti he | udhaaharan: sarkari vibhaagon ko chalaane main hone vaala kharch, sarkari sabsidi, karj par byaaj kii adaayagi, rajya sarkaron ko anudaan aadi |18
 Capital Expenditure: Those expenses of the government are kept under capital expenditure which leads to increase in the assets of the government, such as road, school, hospital, repair of any old building etc
 19
 Planned Expenditure: That expenditure is called plan expenditure from which production assets are produced
 yah vyay vibhinn aarthik kalyankari yojanaon se sambandhit hota he, jaise skool, sadak, hospital kaa nirmaan aadi
 20
 gaiyr yojanagat vyay (non-plan Expenditure):aisa saarvajanik vyay jisase ki koi vikaas kaa kaam nahi hota he, gaiyr yojanagat vyay kii shrenee main gina jaataa he
 Such as expenditure on defense expenditure, pension, dearness allowance, flood, drought, hailstorm etc
 iske liye dhan kii vyavastha bharat kii sanchit nidhi se hoti he
